style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">On July 23, 2015, NorthWestern Corporation d/b/a NorthWestern Energy (NYSE: NWE) (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Company</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;) issued a press release announcing that on July 22, 2015, the Company</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">entered into a definitive agreement (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Agreement</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;) with BayWa r.e. Wind LLC (&#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Seller</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;), to purchase Seller's 100% ownership interest in Beethoven Wind, LLC, which owns Project Beethoven, an 80 megawatt wind farm (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Project</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;) located near Tripp, South Dakota, in Hutchinson, Bon Homme and Charles Mix counties. The purchase price established by the Agreement is $143&#160;million, subject to post-closing adjustments for operating expenses, accounts receivable, and the usage of energy by the Company under existing power purchase agreements between the Company and the Seller pursuant to which the Company currently purchases all of the power generated by the Project.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 hereto and is incorporated herein by reference.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:16px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The Agreement contains customary representations and warranties, covenants, and indemnification obligations. The closing of the acquisition is expected to occur by the end of 2015, and is subject to customary conditions and approvals, including approval from the Federal Energy Regulatory Commission. The foregoing description is not complete, and is qualified by reference to the full text of the Agreement, a copy of which is attached to this Current Report on Form 8-K as Exhibit 2.1 and is incorporated by reference in this Item 1.01 as though it was fully set forth herein.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:16px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The Agreement has been attached as an exhibit to this Current Report on Form 8-K to provide investors and security holders with information regarding its terms. It is not intended to provide any other factual information about the Project or the Company. The representations, warranties, covenants and agreements contained in the Agreement were made only for the purposes of such agreement and as of specified dates, were solely for the benefit of the parties to such agreement, and may be subject to limitations agreed upon by the contracting parties. The representations and warranties may have been made for the purposes of allocating contractual risk between the parties to the Agreement instead of establishing these matters as facts, and may be subject to standards of materiality applicable to the contracting parties that differ from those applicable to investors. Investors and security holders are not third-party beneficiaries under the Agreement and should not rely on the representations, warranties, covenants and agreements or any descriptions thereof as characterizations of the actual state of facts or condition of the Project or the Company. Moreover, the assertions embodied in the representations and warranties contained in the Agreement are qualified by information in disclosure schedules that the parties have exchanged. Accordingly, investors and security holders should not rely on the representations and warranties as characterizations of the actual state of facts of the Project or the Company or its businesses. Information concerning the subject matter of the representations and warranties may change after the date of the Agreement, which subsequent information may or may not be fully reflected in the Company's public disclosures.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:16px;text-align:center;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">SPECIAL NOTE REGARDING FORWARD-LOOKING STATEMENTS</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;padding-top:16px;text-align:left;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">This Current Report on Form 8-K contains forward-looking statements within the meaning of the &#8220;safe harbor&#8221; provisions of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. On the terms and subject to the conditions hereof, on the Closing Date (a)&#160;Seller shall sell, transfer, convey and assign to Buyer, and Buyer shall purchase and acquire from Seller, all of the right, title and interest of Seller in and to the Target Interests free and clear of any and all Liens and (b)&#160;the Parties shall take or cause to be taken the other actions described in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Article 3</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">2.2&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Aggregate Purchase Price</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. The aggregate consideration that Buyer shall pay to Seller for all of the Target Interests shall be an amount equal to $143,000,000 (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Base Purchase Price</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;); </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">plus</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">minus</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;each of the following adjustments, without duplication (collectively, the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Adjustments</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;): (a) </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">minus</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;Unpaid Expenses, (b) </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">plus</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;Prepaid Expenses, (c) </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">plus</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;Accounts Receivable and (d) </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">plus</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;Unbilled Energy Costs, which amount, after all such Adjustments, is collectively referred to herein as the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Aggregate Purchase Price</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;. The Aggregate Purchase Price shall be subject to adjustment subject to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 2.4</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">2.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Estimated Aggregate Purchase Price</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. At least three (3) Business Days prior to the Closing Date, Seller shall deliver to Buyer a statement (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Closing Estimate and Funds Flow Statement</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;)</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">setting forth (i) good faith estimates of the amounts of: the Unpaid Expenses (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Estimated Unpaid Expenses</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;), the Prepaid Expenses (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Estimated Prepaid Expenses</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;), the Accounts Receivable (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Estimated Accounts Receivable</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;) and the Unbilled Energy Costs (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Estimated Unbilled Energy Costs</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;); (ii) the Estimated Aggregate Purchase Price; and (iii) the wire transfer instructions referenced in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 3.2.5</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. The Estimated Aggregate Purchase Price shall be paid to Seller on the Closing Date pursuant to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 3.2.5</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">2.4&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Post-Closing Adjustments</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">2.4.1&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Promptly after the Closing Date, and in any event not later than fifteen (15) days following the Closing Date, Buyer shall prepare and deliver to Seller a written statement (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Closing Statement</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;) which shall set forth in reasonable detail (a) Buyer&#8217;s good faith calculations of (i) the actual amount of any Unpaid Expenses not paid by or on behalf of the Project Company on or prior to the Closing Date, (ii) the actual amount of the Prepaid Expenses, (iii) the actual amount of the Accounts Receivable and (iv) the actual amount of the Unbilled Energy Costs and (b) Buyer&#8217;s calculation of the Aggregate Purchase Price based on the Buyer&#8217;s recalculations of the Adjustments contained in the Closing Statement (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Buyer&#8217;s Proposed Calculations</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;). The Closing Statement shall quantify in reasonable detail the items constituting the calculations of the Unpaid Expenses, the Prepaid Expenses, the Accounts </font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sc2e63d4b93974295bc906187833d9018"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Receivable and the Unbilled Energy Costs included therein using the same line items and detail (to the extent applicable) that was set forth in the Closing Estimate and Funds Flow Statement and, in each case, calculated in accordance with the terms of this Agreement.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">2.4.2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Buyer shall provide a reasonable level of supporting documentation for the Closing Statement. Prior to and following delivery by Buyer of the Closing Statement, Buyer shall provide Seller and its Representatives with prompt and reasonable access to the books and records of Buyer reasonably requested by Seller in order to allow Seller to verify the accuracy of the Buyer&#8217;s Proposed Calculations.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">2.4.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">In the event that Seller does not object to Buyer&#8217;s Proposed Calculations by written notice of objection (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Notice of Objection</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;) delivered to Buyer within five (5) days after Seller&#8217;s receipt of the Closing Statement, the calculation of the Aggregate Purchase Price as set forth in Buyer&#8217;s Proposed Calculations shall be deemed final and binding. The Notice of Objection, if any, shall set forth, in reasonable detail: (a) Seller&#8217;s alternative calculations of (i) the actual amount of any Unpaid Expenses not paid by or on behalf of the Project Company on or prior to the Closing Date, (ii) the actual amount of the Prepaid Expenses, (iii) the actual amount of the Accounts Receivable and (iv) the actual amount of the Unbilled Energy Costs; and (b) Seller&#8217;s alternative recalculation of the Adjustments contained in the Notice of Objection, in each case calculated in accordance with the terms of this Agreement (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Seller&#8217;s Proposed Calculations</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;).</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">2.4.4&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">If Seller delivers a Notice of Objection to Buyer within the 5-day period referred to in </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 2.4.3</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, then (x) any amount of Buyer&#8217;s Proposed Calculations that is not in dispute on the date such Notice of Objection is given shall be treated as final and binding and (y) any dispute with respect to Buyer&#8217;s Proposed Calculations (all such disputed amounts, the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Disputed Amounts</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;) shall be resolved as follows:</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Seller and Buyer shall promptly endeavor in good faith to resolve the Disputed Amounts listed in the Notice of Objection. In the event that a written agreement between the Parties determining the Disputed Amounts has not been reached within thirty (30) days after the date of receipt by Buyer from Seller of the Notice of Objection, Seller and Buyer shall select a mutually acceptable and nationally recognized independent accounting firm (such firm, the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Independent Accounting Firm</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;) to resolve the Disputed Amounts in accordance with the provisions of this </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 2.4</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. The Parties acknowledge that PricewaterhouseCoopers is a mutually acceptable firm to be designated as the Independent Accounting Firm.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The Independent Accounting Firm shall conduct its own review and verification, based solely upon written submissions by Buyer and Seller (and not upon an independent review), of only those items set forth on the Seller&#8217;s Proposed Calculations that remain Disputed Amounts after the Parties&#8217; efforts pursuant to clause (a) of this </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 2.4.4</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, and shall select either Buyer&#8217;s Proposed Calculations of the Disputed Amounts or Seller&#8217;s Proposed Calculations of the Disputed Amounts or an amount that is between the two proposed calculations.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Seller and Buyer shall use their commercially reasonable efforts to cause the Independent Accounting Firm to render a decision in accordance with this </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 2.4</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, along with a statement of reasons therefor, within thirty (30) days of the submission of the Disputed Amounts to the Independent Accounting Firm or a reasonable time thereafter. The decision of the Independent Accounting Firm shall be final and binding upon Seller and Buyer and the decision of the Independent Accounting Firm shall constitute an arbitral award that is final, binding and non-appealable and upon which a judgment may be entered by a court having jurisdiction thereover, absent manifest calculation error.</font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sc2e63d4b93974295bc906187833d9018"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;In the event Seller and Buyer submit any Disputed Amounts to the Independent Accounting Firm for resolution, (i) Seller and Buyer shall each pay their own costs and expenses incurred under this </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 2.4</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">; and (ii) the fees and expenses of the Independent Accounting Firm shall be borne by the Party that is not the substantially prevailing Party, as determined by the Independent Accounting Firm based on the Independent Accounting Firm&#8217;s resolution of the issues.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">2.4.5&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The Independent Accounting Firm shall act as an arbitrator to determine, based upon the provisions of this </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 2.4</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, only the Disputed Amounts. The Independent Accounting Firm&#8217;s determination of each amount of the Disputed Amounts shall be made in accordance with the procedures set forth in </font><font Seller is qualified to conduct business in all jurisdictions where the failure to qualify would materially and adversely affect its ability to execute or deliver, or perform its obligations under, the Transaction Documents to which it is a party. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">4.1.2&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Authority and Power</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. (x) Except as set forth on </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Schedule 4.1.4</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, as of the date hereof, and (y) as of the Closing Date, the execution, delivery and performance of each of the Transaction Documents to which Seller is a party and the consummation of each of the transactions and undertakings contemplated thereby have been duly authorized by all requisite action on the part of Seller and its members under its Charter Documents.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">4.1.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Valid and Binding Obligations</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Seller is not an &#8220;investment company&#8221; or a company controlled by an &#8220;investment company&#8221; within the meaning of the Investment Company Act of 1940.</font></div><div Governmental Person or the staff or regulators of any Governmental Person, with such notice being sufficient to provide the other Party with the opportunity to attend and participate in such meeting, style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Tax Matters</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.2.1&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Tax Indemnity</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;To the fullest extent permitted by applicable Law, Seller shall defend, indemnify and hold harmless Buyer and its Affiliates (including the Project Company) and their respective partners, managers, members, shareholders, consultants, Representatives, successors and assigns from and against any Loss suffered or incurred by such Persons to the extent arising out of, or resulting from (i)&#160;Seller Taxes, (ii)&#160;any liability of the Project Company for the Taxes of any other Person under Section&#160;1.1502-6 of the Treasury Regulations (or any similar provision of state, local or foreign Law) as a result of having been a member of a consolidated, affiliated, combined or unitary group prior to the Closing and (iii)&#160;any breach of any representation, warranty or covenant of Seller (or any Affiliate thereof) in this Agreement relating to Taxes.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Except as otherwise provided in this Agreement, to the fullest extent permitted by applicable Law, Buyer shall defend, indemnify and hold harmless Seller and its Affiliates and their respective partners, managers, members, shareholders, consultants, Representatives, successors and assigns from and against any Loss suffered or incurred by such Persons to the extent arising out of, or resulting from (i)&#160;any Tax of the Project Company relating to a taxable period beginning after the Closing Date and that portion of any Straddle Period beginning after the Closing Date (as determined under </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.3</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">) and (ii)&#160;all Taxes of Buyer and all Affiliates thereof, including the Project Company but only relating to a taxable period beginning after the Closing Date and that portion of any Straddle Period beginning after the Closing Date.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Whenever Seller or Buyer shall be required to pay the other party an amount with respect to this </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, such payments shall be made no later than ten (10)&#160;days after such payments are requested.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.2.2&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Tax Returns</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Subject to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.2(b)</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, with respect to any Tax Return covering a Pre-Closing Taxable Period that is required to be filed with respect to the Project Company, (i)&#160;Seller shall cause such Tax Return to be prepared in compliance with applicable Law and in a manner consistent with practices followed in prior taxable periods to the extent permitted by applicable Law and shall deliver such Tax Return to Buyer, for its review at least forty-five (45)&#160;days prior to the due date (including valid extensions) for filing such Tax Return, (ii)&#160;Seller and Buyer shall cooperate and consult with each other to finalize such Tax Return and Seller shall incorporate any reasonable comments proposed by Buyer, and (iii)&#160;Seller shall cause such Tax Return to be executed and filed within the time and in the manner required by applicable Law with the appropriate Taxing Authority and shall pay all Taxes shown as due and payable on such Tax Return or otherwise payable, in each case, within the time and in the manner required by applicable Law.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sc2e63d4b93974295bc906187833d9018"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;With respect to any Tax Return covering a Straddle Period that is required to be filed after the Closing Date with respect to the Project Company, (i)&#160;Buyer shall cause such Tax Return to be prepared in compliance with applicable Law and shall deliver a draft of such Tax Return to Seller, for its review at least forty-five (45)&#160;days prior to the due date (including valid extensions) for filing such Tax Return, (ii)&#160;Seller and Buyer shall cooperate and consult with each other in order to finalize such Tax Return and Buyer shall incorporate any reasonable comments proposed by Seller, and (iii)&#160;at least five (5)&#160;days prior to the due date (including valid extensions) for filing such Tax Return, Seller shall pay to Buyer the portion of any Taxes shown as due and payable on such Tax Return with respect to the portion of the period that ends on the Closing Date (as determined under </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.3</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">), and (iv)&#160;Buyer shall cause such Tax Return to be executed and filed within the time and in the manner required by applicable Law with the appropriate Taxing Authority and shall pay all Taxes shown as due and payable on such Tax Return.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.2.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Straddle Period Taxes</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;For purposes of determining the portion of Taxes for any Straddle Period allocable to the Pre-Closing Taxable Period, the portion of any Tax that is allocable to the portion of the period ending as of the end of the Closing Date shall be (i)&#160;in the case of any Taxes other than Taxes based upon or related to income or receipts, the amount of such Tax for the entire taxable period multiplied by a fraction the numerator of which is the number of days in the taxable period ending on the Closing Date and the denominator of which is the number of days in the entire taxable period, and (ii)&#160;in the case of any Taxes based upon or related to income or receipts, the amount which would be payable if the relevant taxable period ended on the Closing Date (at the time of the Closing). For purposes of any Taxes payable in arrears on or prior to the Closing Date, all such Taxes shall be the sole responsibility of Seller. For purposes of any Taxes payable in arrears after the Closing Date, all such Taxes shall be apportioned to the Pre-Closing Taxable Period based on the first sentence of this </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.3(a)</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Any Tax credits, including, without limitation, PTCs, relating to a Pre-Closing Taxable Period shall be taken into account as though the relevant taxable period ended on the Closing Date (at the time of the Closing, and, in the case of PTCs, based on appropriate meter readings). All determinations necessary to give effect to the foregoing allocations shall be made in a manner consistent with the prior practices of the Project Company.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.2.4&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Assistance; Books and Records</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Buyer, the Project Company and Seller shall provide each other with such assistance as may reasonably be requested by the others in connection with the preparation of any Tax Return, any audit or other examination by any Governmental Person, or any judicial or administrative proceedings relating to liabilities for Taxes. Such assistance shall include the retention and (upon the other Party&#8217;s reasonable request) the provision of records and information, including copies of Tax Return workpapers and supporting documentation of the Project Company in the possession or control of Seller for any Tax year including or ending prior to the Closing Date which are reasonably relevant to any such proceeding, and making employees and agents available on a mutually convenient basis to provide additional information or explanation of material provided hereunder and shall include providing copies of relevant Tax Returns and supporting material. The Party requesting assistance hereunder shall reimburse the assisting Party for reasonable out of pocket expenses incurred in providing assistance. Buyer, the Project Company and Seller will (a)&#160;retain such Books and Records for the full period of any statute of limitations (and, to the extent notified by Buyer or Seller, any extensions thereof) of the respective taxable periods, (b)&#160;abide by all record retention agreements entered into with any Governmental Person to which the Party is a party, (c)&#160;provide the others with access to any records or information which may be relevant to such preparation, audit, examination, proceeding or </font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sc2e63d4b93974295bc906187833d9018"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">determination upon reasonable request and (d)&#160;with respect to any such Books and Records relating to periods for which the statute of limitations has expired, retain such Books and Records as requested in writing by the other Party (or turn over such Books and Records to such other Party in lieu of retention).</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.2.5&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Audits; Tax Proceedings</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;After the Closing Date, Buyer and Seller shall each notify the other in writing within ten (10)&#160;Business Days of the commencement of any audit or administrative or judicial proceeding affecting the Taxes, Tax attributes or Tax benefits of the Project Company, which, if determined adversely to the taxpayer or after the lapse of time could be grounds for claim under this Agreement against the other Party (such other Party, the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Tax Indemnitor</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;). Such written notice shall contain all material factual information describing any asserted Tax liability in reasonable detail and shall include copies of any notice or other document received from any Governmental Person in respect of any such asserted Tax liability. If either Buyer or Seller fails to give the other Party prompt notice of an asserted Tax liability as required under this Agreement, then the Tax Indemnitor&#8217;s indemnification obligations pursuant to this Agreement shall be limited solely to the extent the Tax Indemnitor is actually prejudiced by such failure. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Seller shall, at its sole cost and expense, have the right to control the contest of any assessment, proposal, claim, reassessment, demand or other Tax proceedings (a &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Tax Contest</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;) that relates solely to a Pre-Closing Taxable Period of the Project Company and that would not be reasonably expected to have an adverse effect on Buyer or the Project Company in any taxable period beginning on or after the Closing Date (a &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Pre-Closing Tax Contest</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;).  In order to exercise its right to control a Pre-Closing Tax Contest, Seller shall give written notice to Buyer of its intent to assume control no later than forty-five (45) days after Seller is notified of the Pre-Closing Tax Contest or such earlier date to the extent any further delay would be reasonably expected to have a material adverse effect on Buyer&#8217;s ability to control the Pre-Closing Tax Contest, but, in no event shall Seller be required to provide Buyer with such notice earlier than ten (10) days after Seller is notified of the Pre-Closing Tax Contest.  In the event that Seller assumes control of a Pre-Closing Tax Contest in accordance with this </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.5</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, Buyer shall be entitled to participate in (but not control) the defense of such Pre-Closing Tax Contest with its own counsel and at its sole cost and expense. Seller shall not settle or otherwise resolve such Pre-Closing Tax Contest without the written consent of Buyer, which consent shall not be unreasonably withheld, conditioned or delayed.  If Seller does not assume control of a Pre-Closing Tax Contest, or if Seller assumes control but fails to diligently and in a timely manner proceed toward the resolution of such Pre-Closing Tax Contest,  Buyer may assume control of and defend against a Pre-Closing Tax Contest in such manner as it deems reasonably appropriate, including settling such contest. Buyer shall have the right to control any other Tax Contest of the Project Company; provided, that Seller shall be entitled to participate in the defense of any Tax Contest controlled by Buyer (including a contest for which Seller could have controlled, but did not provide written notice or failed to diligently proceeds pursuant to this </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.5</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">), with its own counsel and at its sole cost and expense solely to the extent the Tax Contest relates to a Pre-Closing Taxable Period or a Tax liability for which Seller may be required to indemnify Buyer. The Project Company may not settle or otherwise resolve any such Tax Contest with respect to any Tax liability for which Seller is required to indemnify Buyer without the prior written approval of Seller, such approval shall not be unreasonably withheld, conditioned or delayed. The Project Company will execute a power of attorney or other document reasonably requested by Seller to permit Seller to control, settle or otherwise resolve a Pre-Closing Tax Contest. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.2.6&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Refunds</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Subject to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.12</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of this Agreement, all refunds for Taxes for a Pre-Closing Taxable Period or with respect to any Tax Returns relating to a Pre-Closing Taxable Period (including the portion of a Pre-Closing Taxable Period that ends on the Closing Date) that include Seller </font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sc2e63d4b93974295bc906187833d9018"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">or the Project Company, whether or not such Tax Returns are due before or after the Closing Date, shall be property of Seller, and such refunds, plus any interest paid by the Governmental Person in connection with the refund, shall be paid to Seller by the Project Company promptly upon receipt. If at any time subsequent to the payment of a Tax refund to Seller, the applicable Governmental Person claims that all, or any portion, of such refund plus interest should be repaid (such amount being hereinafter referred to as the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Disputed Refund Amount</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;), the Project Company shall notify Seller in writing of the position of such Governmental Person in accordance with the provisions of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.5</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;and Seller shall promptly repay the Disputed Refund Amount to the Project Company, which shall promptly pay the Disputed Refund Amount to the appropriate Governmental Person; </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;">provided</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;">however</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, that, if prior repayment of the Disputed Refund Amount is not required in order to contest a claim for repayment by such Governmental Person, then Seller shall have the right to contest any such claim for repayment by such Governmental Person, prior to the repayment being made by Seller, to the same extent that Seller has the right to contest a claim for taxes under </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.5(b)</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Any Tax Contest relating to a Disputed Refund Amount shall be subject to the provisions of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.5</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, and in the event that the Tax Contest is subsequently resolved in favor, in whole or in part, of the Project Company and all, or a portion, of the Disputed Refund Amount is sustained and refunded to the Project Company, the Project Company shall pay the amount so received by Seller. All other refunds for Taxes shall belong to Buyer and such refunds, plus any interest paid by the Governmental Person in connection with the refund, shall be paid to Buyer by Seller, as applicable, promptly upon receipt. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.2.7&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Controlling Tax Provision</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">To the extent there is an inconsistency between a provision in this </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;and another provision in this Agreement, this </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;shall control.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.2.8&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Sale of Assets</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Subject to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.9</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;of this Agreement, each Party agrees that the transactions contemplated by this Agreement shall be, to the extent permitted by applicable Law, treated for U.S. federal, and, where permitted, state and local income Tax purposes as a sale of all of the assets of the Project Company by Seller to Buyer and, except as required by applicable Law, shall file all income Tax Returns consistently with such treatment. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.2.9&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Transfer Taxes</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Notwithstanding any other provision of this Agreement to the contrary, Buyer shall pay all Transfer Taxes, if any, arising out of or in connection with the transactions contemplated by this Agreement and Buyer shall indemnify, defend and hold harmless Seller with respect to such Transfer Taxes. Seller shall prepare and timely file all Tax Returns or other documentation relating to such Transfer Taxes; </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;">provided</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;">however</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, that to the extent required by applicable Law, Buyer will join in the execution of any such Tax Returns or other documents relating to such Transfer Taxes. Seller shall prepare any such Tax Returns in accordance with the Allocation Schedule and shall provide Buyer with copies of each such Tax Return or other document at least thirty (30)&#160;days prior to the date on which such Tax Return or other document is required to be filed and shall incorporate all reasonable comments received from Buyer with respect to such Tax Returns. &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Transfer Taxes</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221; shall mean any and all Transfer Taxes (excluding Taxes measured in whole or in part by net income), including sales, bulk transfer or sales, use, value added, real property, excise, stock, stamp, documentary, filing, recording, permit, license, authorization and similar Taxes, fees, duties, levies, customs, tariffs, imposts, assessments, obligations and charges of the same or of a similar nature to any of the foregoing. Except as may otherwise be required by Law, for purposes of any Transfer Taxes, Seller and Buyer acknowledge and agree that they shall treat the transactions contemplated by this Agreement as a sale of the Target Interests. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.2.10&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Purchase Price Allocation</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The Parties agree that the Base Purchase Price (plus any other consideration relevant under Section&#160;1060 of the Code) will be allocated to the Assets for Tax purposes in accordance with the allocation schedule to be prepared by the Parties no later than five (5) </font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="sc2e63d4b93974295bc906187833d9018"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Business Days prior to the Closing Date and attached hereto as </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Exhibit&#160;E</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;(the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Allocation Schedule</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8221;). If the Base Purchase Price is adjusted pursuant to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Sections 2.4</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;or </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">6.2.1</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Article 7</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;or any other provision of this Agreement, the Parties shall use their best efforts to adjust the allocation set forth on the Allocation Schedule to reflect the Purchase Price adjustment. Buyer and Seller agree (A)&#160;to act in accordance with the Allocation Schedule in the preparation, filing and amendment (if relevant) of all Tax Returns (including IRS Form&#160;8594 and any similar allocation forms under state, local, county or foreign applicable Law); and (B)&#160;not to take any position inconsistent therewith unless required to do so by (a)&#160;a closing agreement, settlement agreement or similar agreement settling a Tax proceeding entered into among Seller, Buyer (or any Affiliate thereof) and the IRS or any other Taxing Authority, or (b)&#160;a final non-appealable order or judgment rendered by a court of competent jurisdiction concluding a Tax Contest. If any Governmental Person challenges any allocation in any IRS Form&#160;8594 (or any similar allocation form under state, local, county or foreign applicable Law) filed or caused to be filed by Buyer or Seller, the Party receiving notice of such challenge shall give the other Party prompt notice of such challenge, and Buyer and Seller shall cooperate in good faith in responding to such challenge in order to preserve the effectiveness of the Allocation Schedule.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;text-indent:96px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.2.11&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Treatment of Indemnity Payments</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font><font Buyer and all payments by Buyer to or for the benefit of Seller under any indemnity provision of this Agreement, as adjustments to the Aggregate Purchase Price, unless otherwise required by applicable Law (taking into account all relevant facts and circumstances underlying such payment), in which case any such payment will be increased by any Tax cost actually incurred by the recipient or reduced by any Tax benefit actually realized by the recipient, as applicable.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font rebate expected to be received with respect to the South Dakota Reinvestment Payment Program (the &#8220;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Rebate</font><font Company (and, after the Closing Date, Buyer shall cause the Project Company to make such payment) promptly following receipt. If, at any time subsequent to the receipt of the Rebate, SDGOED claims that all, or any portion, of the Rebate should be repaid to SDGOED, the Project Company shall notify Seller in writing of such claim in accordance with the provisions of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.5</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Seller shall control the contest of any dispute relating to such claim to the same extent that Seller has the right to contest a claim for Taxes under </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;text-decoration:underline;">Section 6.2.5(b)</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, except that (i) the reference to forty-five (45) days in the second sentence thereof shall be ninety (90) days, and (ii) the consent of Buyer to a settlement or other resolution of the dispute shall not be required if Seller provides funds to the Project Company in an amount equal to any payment that is required to be made to SDGOED under the proposed settlement or other resolution of the dispute. To the extent that all, or a portion, of the Rebate is required to be repaid to SDGOED pursuant to a final settlement or other resolution of such dispute, such amount shall promptly be paid by Seller to the Project Company, and the Project Company shall promptly pay such amount to SDGOED.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.3&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Reliance Letters</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">. Buyer shall be responsible for any Expansion Phase COD Payment (as defined in the B&amp;H PSA) owed to B&amp;H.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;text-indent:48px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">6.10&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Supplements to Disclosure Schedules</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.
